(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($P --> 
        ( [ $M ])) $T1) 
            ( ($S <-> $M) $T2)) 
            ( ($P --> 
                ( [ $S ])) 
                    (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[['{...}',['$A']],<->,['{...}',['$B']]]],[A,<->,B],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( { $A } <-> 
          { $B })) 
            ($A <-> $B) 
            (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[['[...]',['$A']]],<->,[['[...]',['$B']]]]],[A,<->,B],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ( [ $A ]) <-> 
            ( [ $B ]))) 
                ($A <-> $B) 
                (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[['{...}',['$A','$B']],-->,M],T]],[[['{...}',['$A']],-->,M],['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])

  ( ($S --> $M) 
    (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))

  ( ($M --> $S) 
    (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))

        ($S & $P)) $T)) 
  ( ($M --> $P)

  ( ($A --> $M)

;;;!Extensional and intensional intersection composition: (sets via reductions)
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,-->,M],T1],[[S,-->,M],T2]],[[[P,'|',S],-->,M],['Truth_Intersection',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($P --> $M) $T1) 
    ( ($S --> $M) $T2)) 
  ( ( ($P | $S) --> $M) 
    (Truth_Intersection $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,-->,M],T1],[[S,-->,M],T2]],[[[P,&,S],-->,M],['Truth_Union',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($P --> $M) $T1) 
    ( ($S --> $M) $T2)) 
  ( ( ($P & $S) --> $M) 
    (Truth_Union $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,-->,M],T1],[[S,-->,M],T2]],[[[P,~,S],-->,M],['Truth_Difference',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($P --> $M) $T1) 
    ( ($S --> $M) $T2)) 
  ( ( ($P ~ $S) --> $M) 
    (Truth_Difference $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,P],T1],[[M,-->,S],T2]],[[M,-->,[P,&,S]],['Truth_Intersection',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($M --> $P) $T1) 
    ( ($M --> $S) $T2)) 
  ( ($M --> 
      ($P & $S)) 
    (Truth_Intersection $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,P],T1],[[M,-->,S],T2]],[[M,-->,[P,'|',S]],['Truth_Union',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($M --> $P) $T1) 
    ( ($M --> $S) $T2)) 
  ( ($M --> 
      ($P | $S)) 
    (Truth_Union $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,P],T1],[[M,-->,S],T2]],[[M,-->,[P,-,S]],['Truth_Difference',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($M --> $P) $T1) 
    ( ($M --> $S) $T2)) 
  ( ($M --> 
      ($P - $S)) 
    (Truth_Difference $T1 $T2)))


;;;!Extensional and intensional intersection decomposition:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[S,-->,M],T1],[[[S,'|',P],-->,M],T2]],[[P,-->,M],['Truth_DecomposePNN',T1,T2]]])

;;; NAL-4
;;;!Transformation rules between product and image:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T]],[[A,-->,[R,'/1',B]],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T)) 
  ( ($A --> 
      ($R /1 $B)) 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T]],[[B,-->,[R,'/2',A]],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T)) 
  ( ($B --> 
      ($R /2 $A)) 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T]],[[[R,'\\1',B],-->,A],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $B)) $T)) 
  ( ( ($R \1 $B) --> $A) 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T]],[[[R,'\\2',A],-->,B],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $B)) $T)) 
  ( ( ($R \2 $A) --> $B) 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


;;;other direction of same rules (as these are bi-directional)
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,-->,[R,'/1',B]],T]],[[[A,*,B],-->,R],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($A --> 
        ($R /1 $B)) $T)) 
  ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[B,-->,[R,'/2',A]],T]],[[[A,*,B],-->,R],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($B --> 
        ($R /2 $A)) $T)) 
  ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[R,'\\1',B],-->,A],T]],[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($R \1 $B) --> $A) $T)) 
  ( ($R --> 
      ($A * $B)) 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[R,'\\2',A],-->,B],T]],[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($R \2 $A) --> $B) $T)) 
  ( ($R --> 
      ($A * $B)) 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


;;;!Comparative relations
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[['{...}',['$R']],'|-',>,[['[...]',['$P']]]],T1],[[['{...}',['$S']],'|-',>,[['[...]',['$P']]]],T2]],[[[['{...}',['$R']],*,['{...}',['$S']]],-->,[>>>,P]],['Truth_FrequencyGreater',T1,T2]]])

          ( [ $P ])) $T1)

                    ( [ $P ])) $T2))

                                { $S }) --> 
                                  (>>> $P)) 
                                  (Truth_FrequencyGreater $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,[>>>,P]],T1],[[[B,*,C],-->,[>>>,P]],T2]],[[[A,*,C],-->,[>>>,P]],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])

        (>>> $P)) $T2))

      (>>> $P)) 
    (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[['{...}',['$R']],'|-',>,[['[...]',['$P']]]],T1],[[['{...}',['$S']],'|-',>,[['[...]',['$P']]]],T2]],[[[['{...}',['$R']],*,['{...}',['$S']]],-->,[===,P]],['Truth_FrequencyEqual',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( { $R } |- > 
          ( [ $P ])) $T1) 
              ( ( { $S } |- > 
                    ( [ $P ])) $T2)) 
                        ( ( ( { $R } * 
                                { $S }) --> 
                                  (=== $P)) 
                                  (Truth_FrequencyEqual $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,[===,P]],T1],[[[B,*,C],-->,[===,P]],T2]],[[[A,*,C],-->,[===,P]],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|-

      (=== $P))

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,[===,P]],T]],[[[B,*,A],-->,[===,P]],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])

      (=== $P)) 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


;;;!Optional rules for more efficient reasoning about relation components:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[[C,*,B],-->,R],T2]],[[C,-->,A],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
(=

    ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1)

  ( ($C --> $A)

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[[A,*,C],-->,R],T2]],[[C,-->,B],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[A,-->,C],T2]],[[[C,*,B],-->,R],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]]])

    ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1)

    (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[C,<->,A],T2]],[[[C,*,B],-->,R],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
(=

    ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1)

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[C,-->,B],T2]],[[[A,*,C],-->,R],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
(=

    ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1)

    (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[B,-->,C],T2]],[[[A,*,C],-->,R],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
    ( ($B --> $C) $T2)) 
  ( ( ($A * $C) --> $R) 
    (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[C,<->,B],T2]],[[[A,*,C],-->,R],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
    ( ($C <-> $B) $T2)) 
  ( ( ($A * $C) --> $R) 
    (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[A,-->,C],T2]],[[R,-->,[C,*,B]],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])

    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $B)) $T1)

      ($C * $B)) 
    (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[C,-->,A],T2]],[[R,-->,[C,*,B]],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
(=

    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $B)) $T1) 
    ( ($C --> $A) $T2)) 
  ( ($R --> 
      ($C * $B)) 
    (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[C,<->,A],T2]],[[R,-->,[C,*,B]],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $B)) $T1) 
    ( ($C <-> $A) $T2)) 
  ( ($R --> 
      ($C * $B)) 
    (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[B,-->,C],T2]],[[R,-->,[A,*,C]],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $B)) $T1) 
    ( ($B --> $C) $T2)) 
  ( ($R --> 
      ($A * $C)) 
    (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[C,-->,B],T2]],[[R,-->,[A,*,C]],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $B)) $T1) 
    ( ($C --> $B) $T2)) 
  ( ($R --> 
      ($A * $C)) 
    (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[C,<->,B],T2]],[[R,-->,[A,*,C]],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $B)) $T1) 
    ( ($C <-> $B) $T2)) 
  ( ($R --> 
      ($A * $C)) 
    (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[[C,*,B],-->,R],T2]],[[A,<->,C],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
    ( ( ($C * $B) --> $R) $T2)) 
  ( ($A <-> $C) 
    (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[[A,*,C],-->,R],T2]],[[B,<->,C],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
    ( ( ($A * $C) --> $R) $T2)) 
  ( ($B <-> $C) 
    (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[R,-->,[C,*,B]],T2]],[[A,<->,C],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $B)) $T1) 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($C * $B)) $T2)) 
  ( ($A <-> $C) 
    (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[R,-->,[A,*,C]],T2]],[[B,<->,C],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $B)) $T1) 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $C)) $T2)) 
  ( ($B <-> $C) 
    (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


;;;NAL-5
;;;!Negation conjunction and disjunction decomposition:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[!,A],T]],[A,['Truth_Negation',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( (! $A) $T)) 
  ($A 
    (Truth_Negation $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,&&,B],T]],[A,['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($A && $B) $T)) 
  ($A 
    (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,&&,B],T]],[B,['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($A && $B) $T)) 
  ($B 
    (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,&&,B],T]],[[B,&&,A],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($A && $B) $T)) 
  ( ($B && $A) 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[S,T1],[[S,&&,A],T2]],[A,['Truth_DecomposePNN',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ($S $T1) 
    ( ($S && $A) $T2)) 
  ($A 
    (Truth_DecomposePNN $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[S,T1],[[S,'||',A],T2]],[A,['Truth_DecomposeNPP',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ($S $T1) 
    ( ($S || $A) $T2)) 
  ($A 
    (Truth_DecomposeNPP $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[S,T1],[[[!,S],&&,A],T2]],[A,['Truth_DecomposeNNN',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ($S $T1) 
    ( ( (! $S) && $A) $T2)) 
  ($A 
    (Truth_DecomposeNNN $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[S,T1],[[[!,S],'||',A],T2]],[A,['Truth_DecomposePPP',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ($S $T1) 
    ( ( (! $S) || $A) $T2)) 
  ($A 
    (Truth_DecomposePPP $T1 $T2)))


;;;!Syllogistic rules for Implication:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,B],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[A,==>,C],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($A ==> $B) $T1) 
    ( ($B ==> $C) $T2)) 
  ( ($A ==> $C) 
    (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,B],T1],[[A,==>,C],T2]],[[C,==>,B],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($A ==> $B) $T1) 
    ( ($A ==> $C) $T2)) 
  ( ($C ==> $B) 
    (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,C],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[B,==>,A],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($A ==> $C) $T1) 
    ( ($B ==> $C) $T2)) 
  ( ($B ==> $A) 
    (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,B],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[C,==>,A],['Truth_Exemplification',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($A ==> $B) $T1) 
    ( ($B ==> $C) $T2)) 
  ( ($C ==> $A) 
    (Truth_Exemplification $T1 $T2)))


;;;!Conditional composition for conjunction and disjunction:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,C],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[[A,&&,B],==>,C],['Truth_Union',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($A ==> $C) $T1) 
    ( ($B ==> $C) $T2)) 
  ( ( ($A && $B) ==> $C) 
    (Truth_Union $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,C],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[[A,'||',B],==>,C],['Truth_Intersection',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($A ==> $C) $T1) 
    ( ($B ==> $C) $T2)) 
  ( ( ($A || $B) ==> $C) 
    (Truth_Intersection $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[C,==>,A],T1],[[C,==>,B],T2]],[[C,==>,[A,&&,B]],['Truth_Intersection',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($C ==> $A) $T1) 
    ( ($C ==> $B) $T2)) 
  ( ($C ==> 
      ($A && $B)) 
    (Truth_Intersection $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[C,==>,A],T1],[[C,==>,B],T2]],[[C,==>,[A,'||',B]],['Truth_Union',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($C ==> $A) $T1) 
    ( ($C ==> $B) $T2)) 
  ( ($C ==> 
      ($A || $B)) 
    (Truth_Union $T1 $T2)))


;;;!Multi-conditional inference:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[S,&&,P],==>,M],T1],[[S,==>,M],T2]],[P,['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($S && $P) ==> $M) $T1) 
    ( ($S ==> $M) $T2)) 
  ($P 
    (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[C,&&,M],==>,P],T1],[[S,==>,M],T2]],[[[C,&&,S],==>,P],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($C && $M) ==> $P) $T1) 
    ( ($S ==> $M) $T2)) 
  ( ( ($C && $S) ==> $P) 
    (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[C,&&,P],==>,M],T1],[[[C,&&,S],==>,M],T2]],[[S,==>,P],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($C && $P) ==> $M) $T1) 
    ( ( ($C && $S) ==> $M) $T2)) 
  ( ($S ==> $P) 
    (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[C,&&,M],==>,P],T1],[[M,==>,S],T2]],[[[C,&&,S],==>,P],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($C && $M) ==> $P) $T1) 
    ( ($M ==> $S) $T2)) 
  ( ( ($C && $S) ==> $P) 
    (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2)))


;;;!Rules for equivalence:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[S,<=>,P],T]],[[P,<=>,S],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($S <=> $P) $T)) 
  ( ($P <=> $S) 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[S,==>,P],T1],[[P,==>,S],T2]],[[S,<=>,P],['Truth_Intersection',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($S ==> $P) $T1) 
    ( ($P ==> $S) $T2)) 
  ( ($S <=> $P) 
    (Truth_Intersection $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,==>,M],T1],[[S,==>,M],T2]],[[S,<=>,P],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($P ==> $M) $T1) 
    ( ($S ==> $M) $T2)) 
  ( ($S <=> $P) 
    (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,==>,P],T1],[[M,==>,S],T2]],[[S,<=>,P],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($M ==> $P) $T1) 
    ( ($M ==> $S) $T2)) 
  ( ($S <=> $P) 
    (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,==>,P],T1],[[S,<=>,M],T2]],[[S,==>,P],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($M ==> $P) $T1) 
    ( ($S <=> $M) $T2)) 
  ( ($S ==> $P) 
    (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,==>,M],T1],[[S,<=>,M],T2]],[[P,==>,S],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($P ==> $M) $T1) 
    ( ($S <=> $M) $T2)) 
  ( ($P ==> $S) 
    (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,<=>,P],T1],[[S,<=>,M],T2]],[[S,<=>,P],['Truth_Resemblance',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($M <=> $P) $T1) 
    ( ($S <=> $M) $T2)) 
  ( ($S <=> $P) 
    (Truth_Resemblance $T1 $T2)))


;;;!Higher-order decomposition
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[A,T1],[[A,==>,B],T2]],[B,['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ($A $T1) 
    ( ($A ==> $B) $T2)) 
  ($B 
    (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))

    ( ( ($A && $B) ==> $C) $T2)) 
  ( ($B ==> $C) 
    (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[B,T1],[[A,==>,B],T2]],[A,['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])

    ($B $T1) 
    ( ($A ==> $B) $T2)) 
  ($A 
    (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[A,T1],[[A,<=>,B],T2]],[B,['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ($A $T1) 
    ( ($A <=> $B) $T2)) 
  ($B 
    (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


;;;NAL term reductions
;;;!Extensional intersection, union, conjunction reductions:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[A,&,A],A])
(= 
  ($A & $A) $A)


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[A,'|',A],A])
(= 
  ($A | $A) $A)


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[A,&&,A],A])
(= 
  ($A && $A) $A)


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[A,'||',A],A])
(= 
  ($A || $A) $A)


;;;!Extensional set reductions:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[['{...}',[A]],'|',['{...}',[B]]],['{...}',[A,B]]])
(= 
  ( { $A } | 
      { $B }) 
        { $A $B })


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[['{...}',[A,B]],'|',['{...}',[C]]],['{...}',[[A|B],C]]])
(= 
  ( { $A $B } | 
      { $C }) 
        { (Cons  $A $B) $C })


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[['{...}',[C]],'|',['{...}',[A,B]]],['{...}',[C,[A|B]]]])
(= 
  ( { $C } | 
      { $A $B }) 
        { $C 
          (Cons  $A $B) })


;;;!Intensional set reductions:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[[['[...]',[A]]],&,[['[...]',[B]]]],[['[...]',[A,B]]]])
(= 
  ( ( [ $A ]) & 
        ( [ $B ])) 
            ( [ $A $B ]))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[[['[...]',[A,B]]],&,[['[...]',[C]]]],[['[...]',[[A|B],C]]]])
(= 
  ( ( [ $A $B ]) & 
        ( [ $C ])) 
            ( [ (Cons  $A $B) $C ]))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[[['[...]',[A]]],&,[['[...]',[B,C]]]],[['[...]',[A,[B|C]]]]])
(= 
  ( ( [ $A ]) & 
        ( [ $B $C ])) 
            ( [ $A 
                (Cons  $B $C) ]))


;;;!Reduction for set element copula:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['{...}',[[A|B]]],['{...}',[A,B]]])
(= 
  { (Cons  $A $B) } 
    { $A $B })


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[['[...]',[[A|B]]]],[['[...]',[A,B]]]])
(= 
  ( [ (Cons  $A $B) ]) 
      ( [ $A $B ]))

;;retrieve the best candidate (allows to use tuples / collapse results / spaces as a PQ)
!(bind! &tempbest 
  (new-state Nil))

% DEBUG:   eval('&self',['bind!','&tempbest',['new-state','Nil']],OUT).

    -->(7,eval('&self',['bind!','&tempbest',['new-state','Nil']],RET),depth(0))
      -->(8,eval('&self',['new-state','Nil'],RET),depth(1))
      <--(8,retval('State'('Nil',_213540)))
    <--(7,retval('Empty'))
Deterministic: Empty

!(bind! &tempbestscore 
  (new-state 0))

% DEBUG:   eval('&self',['bind!','&tempbestscore',['new-state',0]],OUT).

    -->(9,eval('&self',['bind!','&tempbestscore',['new-state',0]],RET),depth(0))
      -->(10,eval('&self',['new-state',0],RET),depth(1))
      <--(10,retval('State'(0,_319598)))
    <--(9,retval('Empty'))
Deterministic: Empty

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['BestCandidate',Tuple,EvaluateCandidateFunction,T],[sequential,[[do,['change-state!','&tempbestscore',0]],[do,['change-state!','&tempbest','Nil']],[do,['let*',[[X,[superpose,Tuple]],[Fx,[EvaluateCandidateFunction,X,T]]],[superpose,[['If',[>,Fx,['get-state','&tempbestscore']],[sequential,[['change-state!','&tempbest',X],['change-state!','&tempbestscore',Fx]]]]]]]],['get-state','&tempbest']]]])
(= 
  (BestCandidate $Tuple $EvaluateCandidateFunction $T) 
  (sequential 
    ( (do 
        (change-state! &tempbestscore 0)) 
      (do 
        (change-state! &tempbest Nil)) 
      (do 
        (let* 
          ( ($X 
              (superpose $Tuple)) 
            ($Fx 
              ($EvaluateCandidateFunction $X $T))) 
          (superpose 
            ( (If 
                (> $Fx 
                  (get-state &tempbestscore)) 
                (sequential 
                  ( (change-state! &tempbest $X) 
                    (change-state! &tempbestscore $Fx)))))))) 
      (get-state &tempbest))))

      ($OccT $Ev $Prio)) $T)

    ( (add-atom &belief_events $Ev) 
      (UpdateConcept $Ev $T))))


;;bound the size of the attentional focus for tasks / events
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['BoundEvents',Collection,Threshold,Increment,TargetAmount,T],[sequential,[[do,['let*',[[Ev,['get-atoms',Collection]],[['Event',Sentence,[Time,Evidence,EPrio]],Ev]],['If',[<,['EventPriorityNow',EPrio,T],Threshold],['remove-atom',Collection,Ev]]]],[let,CurrentAmount,['CollapseCardinality',['get-atoms',Collection]],['If',[>,CurrentAmount,TargetAmount],['BoundEvents',Collection,[+,Threshold,Increment],Increment,TargetAmount,T]]]]]])
(= 
  (BoundEvents $Collection $Threshold $Increment $TargetAmount $T) 
  (sequential 
    ( (do 
        (let* 
          ( ($Ev 
              (get-atoms $Collection)) 
            ( (Event $Sentence 
                ($Time $Evidence $EPrio)) $Ev)) 
          (If 
            (< 
              (EventPriorityNow $EPrio $T) $Threshold) 
            (remove-atom $Collection $Ev)))) 
      (let $CurrentAmount 
        (CollapseCardinality 
          (get-atoms $Collection)) 
        (If 
          (> $CurrentAmount $TargetAmount) 
          (BoundEvents $Collection 
            (+ $Threshold $Increment) $Increment $TargetAmount $T))))))

;;revise if there is no evidential overlap, else use higher-confident candidate
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['RevisionAndChoice',['Event',[Term1,[F1,C1]],[eternal,Ev1,EPrio1]],['Event',[Term2,[F2,C2]],[eternal,Ev2,EPrio2]]],[let,ConclusionStamp,['TupleConcat',Ev1,Ev2],['If',['StampDisjoint',ConclusionStamp],['Event',[Term1,['Truth_Revision',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]]],[eternal,ConclusionStamp,[0,0.0]]],['If',[>,C1,C2],['Event',[Term1,[F1,C1]],[eternal,Ev1,[0,0.0]]],['Event',[Term2,[F2,C2]],[eternal,Ev2,[0,0.0]]]]]]])
(=

    (Event 
      ($Term1 
        ($F1 $C1)) 
      (eternal $Ev1 $EPrio1))

      ($Term2

      (eternal $Ev2 $EPrio2))) 
  (let $ConclusionStamp 
    (TupleConcat $Ev1 $Ev2) 
    (If 
      (StampDisjoint $ConclusionStamp) 
      (Event 
        ($Term1 
          (Truth_Revision 
            ($F1 $C1) 
            ($F2 $C2))) 
        (eternal $ConclusionStamp 
          (0 0.0)))

        (> $C1 $C2) 
        (Event 
          ($Term1 
            ($F1 $C1)) 
          (eternal $Ev1 
            (0 0.0))) 
        (Event 
          ($Term2 
            ($F2 $C2)) 
          (eternal $Ev2 
            (0 0.0)))))))


;;;update beliefs in existing concept with the new event or create new concept to enter the new evidence
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['UpdateConcept',NewEvent,T],['let*',[[['Event',[Term,TV],[Time,Evidence,EPrio]],NewEvent],[NewEventEternalized,['Eternalize',NewEvent]],[MatchConcept,['Concept',Term,Belief,BeliefEvent,CPrio]]],[sequential,[[case,[match,'&attentional_focus',MatchConcept,MatchConcept],[[MatchConcept,[sequential,[['remove-atom','&attentional_focus',MatchConcept],['let*',[[RevisedBelief,['RevisionAndChoice',Belief,NewEventEternalized]],[MaxPrio,['If',[>,['EventPriorityNow',EPrio,T],['ConceptPriorityNow',CPrio,T]],EPrio,CPrio]]],['add-atom','&attentional_focus',['Concept',Term,RevisedBelief,NewEvent,MaxPrio]]]]]],['%void%',[case,[match,'&concepts',MatchConcept,MatchConcept],[[MatchConcept,[sequential,[['remove-atom','&concepts',MatchConcept],['add-atom','&attentional_focus',MatchConcept],['UpdateConcept',NewEvent,T]]]],['%void%',['add-atom','&attentional_focus',['Concept',Term,NewEventEternalized,NewEvent,EPrio]]]]]]]]]]]])

  (let* 
    ( ( (Event 
          ($Term $TV) 
          ($Time $Evidence $EPrio)) $NewEvent)

        (Eternalize $NewEvent)) 
      ($MatchConcept 
        (Concept $Term $Belief $BeliefEvent $CPrio))) 
    (sequential 
      ( (case 
          (match &attentional_focus $MatchConcept $MatchConcept) 
          ( ($MatchConcept 
              (sequential 
                ( (remove-atom &attentional_focus $MatchConcept) 
                  (let* 
                    ( ($RevisedBelief 
                        (RevisionAndChoice $Belief $NewEventEternalized)) 
                      ($MaxPrio 
                        (If 
                          (> 
                            (EventPriorityNow $EPrio $T) 
                            (ConceptPriorityNow $CPrio $T)) $EPrio $CPrio))) 
                    (add-atom &attentional_focus 
                      (Concept $Term $RevisedBelief $NewEvent $MaxPrio)))))) 
            (%void% 
              (case 
                (match &concepts $MatchConcept $MatchConcept) 
                ( ($MatchConcept 
                    (sequential 
                      ( (remove-atom &concepts $MatchConcept) 
                        (add-atom &attentional_focus $MatchConcept) 
                        (UpdateConcept $NewEvent $T)))) 
                  (%void% 
                    (add-atom &attentional_focus 
                      (Concept $Term $NewEventEternalized $NewEvent $EPrio))))))))))))

;;;Input procedure
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['AddBeliefEvent',Sentence],['let*',[[[T,EvidentialBase],['GetReasonerState']],[InputEvent,['Event',Sentence,[T,EvidentialBase,[T,1.0]]]]],[do,[sequential,[['EventToFIFO',InputEvent],[let,InducedHypothesis,['TemporalImplicationInduction',['get-state','&FIFO']],['UpdateConcept',InducedHypothesis,T]],['ProcessBeliefEvent',InputEvent,T],['Anticipate',['get-state','&FIFO'],T],['BeliefCycle',T]]]]]])

      ($InputEvent 
        (Event $Sentence 
          ($T $EvidentialBase 
            ($T 1.0))))) 
    (do 
      (sequential 
        ( (EventToFIFO $InputEvent) 
          (let $InducedHypothesis 
            (TemporalImplicationInduction 
              (get-state &FIFO)) 
            (UpdateConcept $InducedHypothesis $T)) 
          (ProcessBeliefEvent $InputEvent $T) 
          (Anticipate 
            (get-state &FIFO) $T) 
          (BeliefCycle $T))))))


;;;Procedural inference (decision making with operation execution and subgoaling)
;;Derived goal event priority
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['SubgoalPriority',EPrio,ConcTV],[*,EPrio,['Truth_Expectation',ConcTV]]])
(= 
  (SubgoalPriority $EPrio $ConcTV) 
  (* $EPrio 
    (Truth_Expectation $ConcTV)))


;;Expectation of an operation is the truth expectation of its desire value
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['OpExpectation',['Decision',[Opname,DVOp],Subgoal],T],['Truth_Expectation',DVOp]])
(= 
  (OpExpectation 
    (Decision 
      ($Opname $DVOp) $Subgoal) $T) 
  (Truth_Expectation $DVOp))


;;Inject executed operation as an event and return its name
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['Execute',Opname],[superpose,[['AddBeliefEvent',[Opname,[1.0,0.9]]],Opname]]])
(= 
  (Execute $Opname) 
  (superpose 
    ( (AddBeliefEvent 
        ($Opname 
          (1.0 0.9))) $Opname)))


;;Add subgoals to the PQ
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['DeriveSubgoals',Options],[do,[let,['Decision',Op,Subgoal],[superpose,Options],['add-atom','&goal_events',Subgoal]]]])
(= 
  (DeriveSubgoals $Options) 
  (do 
    (let 
      (Decision $Op $Subgoal) 
      (superpose $Options) 
      (add-atom &goal_events $Subgoal))))


;;execute the operation which most likely gets the goal achieved in current contexts, and if contexts are not yet fulfilled, derive them as subgoals
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['BestDecision',T,['Event',[Term,DV],[GoalTime,GoalEvBase,GoalPrio]],FIFO],[let,Options,[collapse,['let*',[[['Event',[[[Prec,&/,[^,Op]],=/>,Term],ImpTV],[ImpTime,ImpEvBase,ImpPrio]],['EternalQuestion',[[Prec,&/,[^,Op]],=/>,Term]]],[DVPrecOp,['Truth_Deduction',DV,ImpTV]],[['Event',[PrecTerm,PrecTV],PrecMetadata],['Projection',['EventQuestion',Prec],T]],[DVOp,['Truth_Deduction',PrecTV,DVPrecOp]],[DVPrec,['Truth_StructuralDeduction',DVPrecOp]],[SubgoalStamp,['TupleConcat',GoalEvBase,ImpEvBase]]],['If',['StampDisjoint',SubgoalStamp],['Decision',[[^,Op],DVOp],['Event',[Prec,['Truth_StructuralDeduction',DVPrecOp]],[T,SubgoalStamp,[T,['SubgoalPriority',['EventPriorityNow',GoalPrio,T],DVPrec]]]]]]]],[let,['Decision',[Opname,DVOp],Subgoal],['BestCandidate',Options,'OpExpectation',T],['If',[>,['Truth_Expectation',DVOp],0.5],['Execute',Opname],['DeriveSubgoals',Options]]]]])
(= 
  (BestDecision $T 
    (Event 
      ($Term $DV) 
      ($GoalTime $GoalEvBase $GoalPrio)) $FIFO) 
  (let $Options 
    (collapse 
      (let* 
        ( ( (Event 
              ( ( ($Prec &/ 
                    (^ $Op)) =/> $Term) $ImpTV) 
              ($ImpTime $ImpEvBase $ImpPrio)) 
            (EternalQuestion 
              ( ($Prec &/ 
                  (^ $Op)) =/> $Term))) 
          ($DVPrecOp 
            (Truth_Deduction $DV $ImpTV)) 
          ( (Event 
              ($PrecTerm $PrecTV) $PrecMetadata) 
            (Projection 
              (EventQuestion $Prec) $T)) 
          ($DVOp 
            (Truth_Deduction $PrecTV $DVPrecOp)) 
          ($DVPrec 
            (Truth_StructuralDeduction $DVPrecOp)) 
          ($SubgoalStamp 
            (TupleConcat $GoalEvBase $ImpEvBase))) 
        (If 
          (StampDisjoint $SubgoalStamp) 
          (Decision 
            ( (^ $Op) $DVOp) 
            (Event 
              ($Prec 
                (Truth_StructuralDeduction $DVPrecOp)) 
              ($T $SubgoalStamp 
                ($T 
                  (SubgoalPriority 
                    (EventPriorityNow $GoalPrio $T) $DVPrec)))))))) 
    (let 
      (Decision 
        ($Opname $DVOp) $Subgoal) 
      (BestCandidate $Options OpExpectation $T) 
      (If 
        (> 
          (Truth_Expectation $DVOp) 0.5) 
        (Execute $Opname) 
        (DeriveSubgoals $Options)))))


;;;select the highest priority goal event from the PQ and use it for decision making
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['GoalCycle',T],[sequential,[[let,Ev,['SelectHighestPriorityEvent','&goal_events',T],[sequential,[[do,['remove-atom','&goal_events',Ev]],['BestDecision',T,Ev,['get-state','&FIFO']]]]],[do,['UpdateReasonerState']],[do,['BoundEvents','&goal_events',0.0,0.1,['GoalEventsMax'],T]]]]])
(= 
  (GoalCycle $T) 
  (sequential 
    ( (let $Ev 
        (SelectHighestPriorityEvent &goal_events $T) 
        (sequential 
          ( (do 
              (remove-atom &goal_events $Ev)) 
            (BestDecision $T $Ev 
              (get-state &FIFO))))) 
      (do 
        (UpdateReasonerState)) 
      (do 
        (BoundEvents &goal_events 0.0 0.1 
          (GoalEventsMax) $T)))))


;;;Input procedure
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['AddGoalEvent',Sentence],['let*',[[[T,EvidentialBase],['GetReasonerState']],[InputEvent,['Event',Sentence,[T,EvidentialBase,[T,1.0]]]]],[sequential,[[do,['add-atom','&goal_events',InputEvent]],['GoalCycle',T]]]]])
(= 
  (AddGoalEvent $Sentence) 
  (let* 
    ( ( ($T $EvidentialBase) 
        (GetReasonerState)) 
      ($InputEvent 
        (Event $Sentence 
          ($T $EvidentialBase 
            ($T 1.0))))) 
    (sequential 
      ( (do 
          (add-atom &goal_events $InputEvent)) 
        (GoalCycle $T)))))
